Healthy).\n43\t    Active,\n44\t    /// Node is joining the cluster (being provisioned).\n45\t    Joining,\n46\t    /// Node is draining (graceful shutdown, not accepting new writes).\n47\t    Draining,\n48\t    /// Node has failed (unplanned outage).\n49\t    Failed,\n50\t    /// Node has been removed from the cluster (tracked for migration).\n51\t    Removed,\n52\t}\n53\t\n54\timpl NodeStatus {\n55\t    /// Check if a transition from `self` to `new_status` is valid.\n56\t    ///\n57\t    /// # State Transition Rules\n58\t    ///\n59\t    /// | From | To | Triggered by |\n60\t    /// |------|-----|-------------|\n61\t    /// | (new) | Joining | `POST /_miroir/nodes` |\n62\t    /// | Joining | Active | Migration complete |\n63\t    /// | Active | Draining | `POST /_miroir/nodes/{id}/drain` |\n64\t    /// | Draining | Removed | Migration complete |\n65\t    /// | Active/Draining | Failed | Health check detects |\n66\t    /// | Failed | Active | Health check recovery |\n67\t    /// | Active/Failed | Degraded | Partial health |\n68\t    /// | Degraded | Active | Health restored |\n69\t    pub fn can_transition_to(self, new_status: NodeStatus) -> bool {\n70\t        match (self, new_status) {\n71\t            // Initial state\n72\t            (NodeStatus::Joining, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n73\t\n74\t            // Normal operations\n75\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Draining) => true,\n76\t            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Removed) => true,\n77\t\n78\t            // Failure and recovery\n79\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n80\t            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n81\t            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n82\t\n83\t            // Degradation\n84\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n85\t            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n86\t            (NodeStatus::Degraded, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n87\t\n88\t            // Healthy <-> Active are bidirectional (synonyms)\n89\t            (NodeStatus::Healthy, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n90\t            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Healthy) => true,\n91\t\n92\t            // Same state is always valid\n93\t            (s, t) if s == t => true,\n94\t\n95\t            // All other transitions are invalid\n96\t            _ => false,\n97\t        }\n98\t    }\n99\t\n100\t    /// Returns `true` if the node can accept writes for the given shard.\n101\t    ///\n102\t    /// # Write Eligibility Rules\n103\t    ///\n104\t    /// A node is write-eligible for a shard based on its status:\n105\t    ///\n106\t    /// | Status | Write Eligible | Notes |\n107\t    /// |--------|----------------|-------|\n108\t    /// | Healthy/Active | Yes | Normal operation |\n109\t    /// | Degraded | Yes | Partial failures, still accepting writes |\n110\t    /// | Joining | No | Being provisioned, not yet ready |\n111\t    /// | Draining | Conditional | Only for shards it still owns during migration |\n112\t    /// | Failed | No | Unavailable |\n113\t    /// | Removed | No | No longer in cluster |\n114\t    ///\n115\t    /// The `draining_shard` parameter should be `Some(shard_id)` if the node\n116\t    /// is in `Draining` status and the shard IS being actively migrated off this node\n117\t    /// (use `None` if the shard is not being drained or no shard is being checked).\n118\t    /// When `Some(...)`, the node is NOT eligible for writes.\n119\t    pub fn is_write_eligible_for(self, draining_shard: Option<u32>) -> bool {\n120\t        match self {\n121\t            NodeStatus::Healthy | NodeStatus::Active | NodeStatus::Degraded => true,\n122\t            NodeStatus::Joining | NodeStatus::Failed | NodeStatus::Removed => false,\n123\t            NodeStatus::Draining => !draining_shard.is_some(),\n124\t        }\n125\t    }\n126\t}\n127\t\n128\timpl fmt::Display for NodeStatus {\n129\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n130\t        match self {\n131\t            NodeStatus::Healthy => write!(f, \"healthy\"),\n132\t            NodeStatus::Degraded => write!(f, \"degraded\"),\n133\t            NodeStatus::Active => write!(f, \"active\"),\n134\t            NodeStatus::Joining => write!(f, \"joining\"),\n135\t            NodeStatus::Draining => write!(f, \"draining\"),\n136\t            NodeStatus::Failed => write!(f, \"failed\"),\n137\t            NodeStatus::Removed => write!(f, \"removed\"),\n138\t        }\n139\t    }\n140\t}\n141\t\n142\t/// A single Meilisearch node in the topology.\n143\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n144\tpub struct Node {\n145\t    /// Unique node } else {\n192\t            Err(TransitionError {\n193\t                from: self.status,\n194\t                to: new_status,\n195\t            })\n196\t        }\n197\t    }\n198\t\n199\t    ///       Self {\n245\t            id,\n246\t            nodes: Vec::new(),\n247\t        }\n248\t    }\n249\t\n250\t    /// Add a node to this group.\n251\t    pub fn add_node(&mut self, node_id: NodeId) self.nodes.len()\n265\t    }\n266\t\n267\t    /// Get all healthy nodes in this group, looking them up from the topology.\n268\t    ///\n269\t    /// This requires access to the topology's node map to .filter_map(|node_id| all_nodes.get(node_id))\n274\t            .filter(|node| node.is_healthy())\n275\t            .collect()\n276\t    }\n277\t}\n278\t\n279\t/// Cluster topology: groups, nodes, and add_node(&mut self, node: Node) {\n308\t        let group_id = node.replica_group as usize;\n309\t\n310\t        // Ensure group exists\n311\t        while self.groups.len() <= group_id {\n312\t            self.groups.push(Group::new(self.groups.len() as u32));\n313\t        }\n314\t\n315\t        self.groups[group_id].add_node(node.id.clone());\n316\t        self.nodes.insert(node.id.clone(), node);\n317\t    }\n318\t\n319\t    /// Get a node by ID.\n320\t    pub fn node(&self, id: &NodeId) -> Option<&Node> {\n321\t        self.nodes.get(id)\n322\t    }\n323\t\n324\t    /// Get a mutable Topology management: node registry, groups, and health state.\n\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::fmt;\n\n/// Unique identifier for a node.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Hash, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct NodeId(String);\n\nimpl NodeId {\n    /// Create a new NodeId.\n    pub fn new(id: String) -> Self {\n        Self(id)\n    }\n\n    /// Get the node ID as a string slice.\n    pub fn as_str(&self) -> &str {\n        &self.0\n    }\n}\n\nimpl From<String> for NodeId {\n    fn from(s: String) -> Self {\n        Self(s)\n    }\n}\n\nimpl AsRef<str> for NodeId {\n    fn as_ref(&self) -> &str {\n        &self.0\n    }\n}\n\n/// Health status of a node.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub enum NodeStatus {\n    /// Node is healthy and serving traffic.\n    Healthy,\n    /// Node is degraded (intermittent failures, still serving traffic).\n    Degraded,\n    /// Node is active and fully operational (synonym for Healthy).\n    Active,\n    /// Node is joining the cluster (being provisioned).\n    Joining,\n    /// Node is draining (graceful shutdown, not accepting new writes).\n    Draining,\n    /// Node has failed (unplanned outage).\n    Failed,\n    /// Node has been removed from the cluster (tracked for migration).\n    Removed,\n}\n\nimpl NodeStatus {\n    /// Check if a transition from `self` to `new_status` is valid.\n    ///\n    /// # State Transition Rules\n    ///\n    /// | From | To | Triggered by |\n    /// |------|-----|-------------|\n    /// | (new) | Joining | `POST /_miroir/nodes` |\n    /// | Joining | Active | Migration complete |\n    /// | Active | Draining | `POST /_miroir/nodes/{id}/drain` |\n    /// | Draining | Removed | Migration complete |\n    /// | Active/Draining | Failed | Health check detects |\n    /// | Failed | Active | Health check recovery |\n    /// | Active/Failed | Degraded | Partial health |\n    /// | Degraded | Active | Health restored |\n    pub fn can_transition_to(self, new_status: NodeStatus) -> bool {\n        match (self, new_status) {\n            // Initial state\n            (NodeStatus::Joining, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n\n            // Normal operations\n            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Draining) => true,\n            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Removed) => true,\n\n            // Failure and recovery\n            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n            (NodeStatus::Draining, NodeStatus::Failed) => true,\n            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n\n            // Degradation\n            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n            (NodeStatus::Failed, NodeStatus::Degraded) => true,\n            (NodeStatus::Degraded, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n\n            // Healthy <-> Active are bidirectional (synonyms)\n            (NodeStatus::Healthy, NodeStatus::Active) => true,\n            (NodeStatus::Active, NodeStatus::Healthy) => true,\n\n            // Same state is always valid\n            (s, t) if s == t => true,\n\n            // All other transitions are invalid\n            _ => false,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Returns `true` if the node can accept writes for the given shard.\n    ///\n    /// # Write Eligibility Rules\n    ///\n    /// A node is write-eligible for a shard based on its status:\n    ///\n    /// | Status | Write Eligible | Notes |\n    /// |--------|----------------|-------|\n    /// | Healthy/Active | Yes | Normal operation |\n    /// | Degraded | Yes | Partial failures, still accepting writes |\n    /// | Joining | No | Being provisioned, not yet ready |\n    /// | Draining | Conditional | Only for shards it still owns during migration |\n    /// | Failed | No | Unavailable |\n    /// | Removed | No | No longer in cluster |\n    ///\n    /// The `draining_shard` parameter should be `Some(shard_id)` if the node\n    /// is in `Draining` status and the shard IS being actively migrated off this node\n    /// (use `None` if the shard is not being drained or no shard is being checked).\n    /// When `Some(...)`, the node is NOT eligible for writes.\n    pub fn is_write_eligible_for(self, draining_shard: Option<u32>) -> bool {\n        match self {\n            NodeStatus::Healthy | NodeStatus::Active | NodeStatus::Degraded => true,\n            NodeStatus::Joining | NodeStatus::Failed | NodeStatus::Removed => false,\n            NodeStatus::Draining => !draining_shard.is_some(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for NodeStatus {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            NodeStatus::Healthy => write!(f, \"healthy\"),\n            NodeStatus::Degraded => write!(f, \"degraded\"),\n            NodeStatus::Active => write!(f, \"active\"),\n            NodeStatus::Joining => write!(f, \"joining\"),\n            NodeStatus::Draining => write!(f, \"draining\"),\n            NodeStatus::Failed => write!(f, \"failed\"),\n            NodeStatus::Removed => write!(f, \"removed\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A single Meilisearch node in the topology.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Node {\n    /// Unique node identifier.\n    pub id: NodeId,\n\n    /// Node base URL / address.\n    pub address: String,\n\n    /// Current health status.\n    pub status: NodeStatus,\n\n    /// Replica group assignment (0-based).\n    pub replica_group: u32,\n}\n\nimpl Node {\n    /// Create a new node.\n    pub fn new(id: NodeId, address: String, replica_group: u32) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            id,\n            address,\n            status: NodeStatus::Joining,\n            replica_group,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Create a new node with a specific status.\n    pub fn with_status(id: NodeId, address: String, replica_group: u32, status: NodeStatus) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            id,\n            address,\n            status,\n            replica_group,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the node is healthy (can serve traffic).\n    pub fn is_healthy(&self) -> bool {\n        matches!(self.status, NodeStatus::Healthy | NodeStatus::Active)\n    }\n\n    /// Transition the node to a new status, validating the transition.\n    ///\n    /// Returns `Ok(())` if the transition is valid, `Err` otherwise.\n    pub fn set_status(&mut self, new_status: NodeStatus) -> Result<(), TransitionError> {\n        if self.status.can_transition_to(new_status) {\n            self.status = new_status;\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            Err(TransitionError {\n                from: self.status,\n                to: new_status,\n            })\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the node is eligible to receive writes for a specific shard.\n    ///\n    /// For nodes in `Draining` status, this depends on whether the shard is\n    /// being actively migrated off this node. The caller should pass\n    /// `Some(shard_id)` if the shard is being drained from this node.\n    pub fn is_write_eligible_for(&self, shard_id: Option<u32>) -> bool {\n        self.status.is_write_eligible_for(shard_id)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Error returned when an invalid state transition is attempted.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub struct TransitionError {\n    pub from: NodeStatus,\n    pub to: NodeStatus,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for TransitionError {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(\n            f,\n            \"invalid state transition from {} to {}\",\n            self.from, self.to\n        )\n    }\n}\n\nimpl std::error::Error for TransitionError {}\n\n/// A replica group: an independent query pool.\n///\n/// Each group holds all S shards, distributed across its nodes.\n/// Reads are routed to a single group per query.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Group {\n    /// Group identifier (0-based).\n    pub id: u32,\n\n    /// Nodes in this group.\n    nodes: Vec<NodeId>,\n}\n\nimpl Group {\n    /// Create a new group.\n    pub fn new(id: u32) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            id,\n            nodes: Vec::new(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Add a node to this group.\n    pub fn add_node(&mut self, node_id: NodeId) {\n        if !self.nodes.contains(&node_id) {\n            self.nodes.push(node_id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the node IDs in this group.\n    pub fn nodes(&self) -> &[NodeId] {\n        &self.nodes\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of nodes in this group.\n    pub fn node_count(&self) -> usize {\n        self.nodes.len()\n    }\n\n    /// Get all healthy nodes in this group, looking them up from the topology.\n    ///\n    /// This requires access to the topology's node map to resolve NodeIds to Nodes.\n    pub fn healthy_nodes<'a>(&'a self, all_nodes: &'a HashMap<NodeId, Node>) -> Vec<&'a Node> {\n        self.nodes\n            .iter()\n            .filter_map(|node_id| all_nodes.get(node_id))\n            .filter(|node| node.is_healthy())\n            .collect()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Cluster topology: groups, nodes, and health state.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct Topology {\n    /// All nodes in the cluster.\n    nodes: HashMap<NodeId, Node>,\n\n    /// Replica groups.\n    groups: Vec<Group>,\n\n    /// Replication factor (intra-group).\n    rf: usize,\n\n    /// Total number of logical shards (S).\n    shards: u32,\n}\n\nimpl Topology {\n    /// Create a new empty topology.\n    pub fn new(shards: u32, rf: usize) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            nodes: HashMap::new(),\n            groups: Vec::new(),\n            rf,\n            shards,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Add a node to the topology.\n    pub fn add_node(&mut self, node: Node) {\n        let group_id = node.replica_group as usize;\n\n        // Ensure group exists\n        while self.groups.len() <= group_id {\n            self.groups.push(Group::new(self.groups.len() as u32));\n        }\n\n        self.groups[group_id].add_node(node.id.clone());\n        self.nodes.insert(node.id.clone(), node);\n    }\n\n    /// Get a node by ID.\n    pub fn node(&self, id: &NodeId) -> Option<&Node> {\n        self.nodes.get(id)\n    }\n\n    /// Get a mutable reference to a node by ID.\n    pub fn node_mut(&mut self, id: &NodeId) -> Option<&mut Node> {\n        self.nodes.get_mut(id)\n    }\n\n    /// Get all nodes.\n    pub fn nodes(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Node> {\n        self.nodes.values()\n    }\n\n    /// Get a group by ID.\n    pub fn group(&self, id: u32) -> Option<&Group> {\n        self.groups.get(id as usize)\n    }\n\n    /// Iterate over all groups.\n    pub fn groups(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Group> {\n        self.groups.iter()\n    }\n\n    /// Get the replication factor.\n    pub fn rf(&self) -> usize {\n        self.rf\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of shards.\n    pub fn shards(&self) -> u32 {\n        self.shards\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of replica groups.\n    pub fn replica_group_count(&self) -> u32 {\n        self.groups.len() as u32\n    }\n\n    /// Get healthy nodes in a specific group.\n    pub fn healthy_nodes_in_group(&self, group_id: u32) -> Vec<&Node> {\n        self.group(group_id)\n            .map(|g| g.healthy_nodes(&self.nodes))\n            .unwrap_or_default()\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    // --- Existing tests updated for address field ---\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_node_is_healthy() {\n        let mut node = Node::new(\n            NodeId::new(\"node1\".to_string()),\n            \"http://example.com\".to_string(),\n            0,\n        );\n\n        // Joining status is not healthy\n        assert!(!node.is_healthy());\n\n        // Healthy status is healthy\n        node.status = NodeStatus::Healthy;\n        assert!(node.is_healthy());\n\n        // Active status is healthy (synonym for Healthy)\n        node.status = NodeStatus::Active;\n        assert!(node.is_healthy());\n\n        // Degraded status is not healthy (intermittent failures)\n        node.status = NodeStatus::Degraded;\n        assert!(!node.is_healthy());\n\n        // Rendezvous hash-based routing and shard assignment.\n2\t\n3\tuse crate::topology::{Group, NodeId, Topology};\n4\tuse std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};\n5\tuse twox_hash::XxHash64;\n6\t\n7\t/// Compute a rendezvous score for a shard+node pair.\n8\t///\n9\t/// Higher scores win; used for deterministic shard assignment.\n10\t///\n11\t/// CRITICAL: Uses seed 0 to match Meilisearch Enterprise's hash function.\n12\t/// Any deviation (different seed, different ordering, endianness) forks\n13\t/// routing across any two Miroir instances and silently corrupts writes.\n14\tpub fn score(shard_id: u32, node_id: &str) -> u64 {\n15\t    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n16\t    shard_id.hash(&mut h);\n17\t    node_id.hash(&mut h);\n18\t    h.finish()\n19\t}\n20\t\n21\t/// Assign a shard to `rf` nodes within a single replica group.\n22\t///\n23\t/// `group_nodes` is the subset of nodes belonging to that group.\n24\t///\n25\t/// Nodes are sorted by score descending, with ties broken lexicographically\n26\t/// by node_id to ensure deterministic assignment even when hash scores collide.\n27\tpub fn assign_shard_in_group(shard_id: u32, group_nodes: &[NodeId], rf: usize) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n28\t    let mut scored: Vec<(u64, &NodeId)> = group_nodes\n29\t        .iter()\n30\t        .map(|n| (score(shard_id, n.as_str()), n))\n31\t        .collect();\n32\t    scored.sort_unstable_by(|a, b| {\n33\t        b.0.cmp(&a.0)\n34\t            .then_with(|| a.1.as_str().cmp(b.1.as_str()))\n35\t    });\n36\t    scored\n37\t        .into_iter()\n38\t        .take(rf)\n39\t        .map(|(_, n)| n.clone())\n40\t        .collect()\n41\t}\n42\t\n43\t/// All write targets for a document: the RF nodes in EACH replica group.\n44\tpub fn write_targets(shard_id: u32, topology: &Topology) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n45\t    topology\n46\t        .groups()\n47\t        .flat_map(|group| assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf()))\n48\t        .collect()\n49\t}\n50\t\n51\t/// Select the replica group for a query (round-robin by query counter).\n52\tpub fn query_group(query_seq: u64, replica_groups: u32) -> u32 {\n53\t    (query_seq % replica_groups as u64) as u32\n54\t}\n55\t\n56\t/// The covering set for a search: one node per shard within the chosen group.\n57\t///\n58\t/// Returns a Vec where index i contains the node to query for shard i.\n59\t/// The length is always exactly shard_count, even if multiple shards\n60\t/// map to the same node.\n61\tpub fn covering_set(shard_count: u32, group: &Group, rf: usize, query_seq: u64) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n62\t    (0..shard_count)\n63\t        .map(|shard_id| {\n64\t            let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n65\t            // rotate through replicas for intra-group load balancing\n66\t            replicas[(query_seq as usize) % replicas.len()].clone()\n67\t        })\n68\t        .collect()\n69\t}\n70\t\n71\t/// Compute the shard ID for a document's primary key.\n72\tpub fn shard_for_key(primary_key: &str, shard_count: u32) -> u32 {\n73\t    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n74\t    primary_key.hash(&mut h);\n75\t    (h.finish() % shard_count as u64) as u32\n76\t}\n77\t\n78\t#[cfg(test)]\n79\tmod tests {\n80\t    use super::*;\n81\t    use crate::topology::{Node, NodeId};\n82\t\n83\t    // Test 1: Rendezvous assignment is set_3.intersection(&set_4).count();\n216\t            if intersection < rf {\n217\t                changed_count += 1;\n218\t            }\n219\t        }\n220\t\n221\t        // Adding a 4th node = (shard_count as f64 * 0.6).ceil() as usize;\n225\t        assert!(\n226\t            changed_count <= max_expected,\n227\t            \"Expected ≤ {max_expected} shards to change, but {changed_count} changed\"\n228\t        );\n229\t\n230\t        // Also verify that not everything changed\n231\t        let min_expected = (shard_count as f64 * 0.2).ceil() as usize;\n232\t        assert!(\n233\t            changed_count >= min_expected,\n234\t            \"Expected at least {min_expected} shards to change, but only {changed_count} changed\"\n235\t        );\n236\t    }\n237\t\n238\t    // Test 7: write_targets returns exactly RG × RF nodes\n239\t    #[test]\n240\t    fn test_write_targets_count() {\n241\t        let mut topology = Topology::new(64, 2); // 64 );\n251\t                topology.add_node(node);\n252\t            }\n253\t        }\n254\t\n255\t        let shard_id = 42;\n256\t        let targets = write_targets(shard_id, {\n283\t        let replica_groups = 3u32;\n284\t        let queries = 1000u64;\n285\t\n286\t        let mut counts = vec![0; replica_groups as usize];\n287\t        for seq in 0..queries {\n288\t            let group = query_group(seq, replica_groups);\n289\t            counts[group as usize] += 1;\n290\t        }\n291\t\n292\t        // Each group should get roughly the same number of            );\n302\t        }\n303\t    }\n304\t\n305\t    // Test 9: covering_set returns exactly one node per shard\n306\t    #[test]\n307\t    fn test_covering_set_one_per_shard() {\n308\t      // Add 3 nodes to a single group\n345\t        for node_idx in 0..3 {\n346\t            let node = Node::new(\n347\t                NodeId::new(format!(\"node-{node_idx}\")),\n348\t (shard_id, nodes) → identical Vec<NodeId> across 1000 randomized runs\n539\t    #[test]\n540\t    fn acceptance_determinism_1000_runs() {\n541\t        let nodes: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n542\t            .into_iter()\n543\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n544\t            .collect();\n545\t\n546\t        for run in 0..1000 {\n547\t            let shard_id = (run % 100) as u32; // Test different shard IDs\n548\t            let rf = ((run % 3) + 1) as usize; // Test different RF values\n549\t\n550\t            let assignment1 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes, rf);\n551\t            let assignment2 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes, rf);\n552\t\n553\t            assert_eq!(\n554\t                assignment1, AT-2: Reshuffle bound on add: 64 shards, 3→4 nodes → at most 2 × (1/4) × 64 edges differ\n562\t    #[test]\n563\t    fn acceptance_reshuffle_bound_on_add() {\n564\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n565\t            .into_iter()\n566\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n567\t            .collect();\n568\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n569\t            .into_iter()\n570\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n571\t            .collect();\n572\t\n573\t        let shard_count = 64;\n574\t        let rf = 1;\n575\t\n576\t        let mut moved_count = 0;\n577\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n578\t            let assign_3 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_3, rf);\n579\t            let assign_4 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_4, rf);\n580\t\n581\t            // Shard moved if its primary owner changed\n582\t            if assign_3.first() != assign_4.first() {\n583\t                moved_count += 1;\n584\t            }\n585\t        }\n586\t\n587\t        // Expected: at most 2 × (1/4) × 64 = 32 edges differ\n588\t        let max_expected = (2.0 * (1.0 / 4.0) * shard_count as f64).ceil() as usize;\n589\t        assert!(\n590\t            moved_count <= max_expected,\n591\t            \"Expected ≤ {max_expected} shard-node edges to differ, but {moved_count} differed\"\n592\t        );\n593\t    }\n594\t\n595\t    // AT-3: Reshuffle bound on remove: 64 shards, 4→3 nodes → ~RF × S / Ng edges differ\n596\t    #[test]\n597\t    fn acceptance_reshuffle_bound_on_remove() {\n598\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n599\t            .into_iter()\n600\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n601\t            .collect();\n602\t        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n603\t            .into_iter()\n604\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n605\t            .collect();\n606\t\n607\t        let shard_count = 64;\n608\t        let rf = 2;\n609\t\n610\t        let mut moved_count = 0;\n611\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n612\t            let assign_4 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_4, rf);\n613\t            let assign_3 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_3, rf);\n614\t\n615\t            // Count edges that differ\n616\t            let set_4: std::collections::HashSet<_> = assign_4.iter().collect();\n617\t            let set_3: std::collections::HashSet<_> = assign_3.iter().collect();\n618\t\n619\t            // An edge differs if it's not in both sets\n620\t            let diff = set_4.symmetric_difference(&set_3).count();\n621\t            if diff > 0 {\n622\t                moved_count += diff;\n623\t            }\n624\t        }\n625\t\n626\t        // Expected: ~RF × S / Ng = 2 × 64 / 4 = 32 edges differ\n627\t        // Allow some variance due to hash distribution\n628\t        let expected = (rf * shard_count as usize) / 4;\n629\t        let tolerance = (expected as f64 * 0.9).ceil() as usize; // ±90%\n630\t        assert!(\n631\t            moved_count >= expected - tolerance && moved_count <= expected + tolerance,\n632\t            \"Expected ~{expected} shard-node edges to differ (±{tolerance}), but {moved_count} differed\"\n633\t        );\n634\t    }\n635\t\n636\t    // AT-4: Uniformity: 64 shards, 3 nodes, RF=1 → each node holds 15–27 shards\n637\t    #[test]\n638\t    fn acceptance_uniformity_64_shards_3_nodes_rf1() {\n639\t        let nodes: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n640\t            .into_iter()\n641\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n642\t            .collect();\n643\t        let shard_count = 64;\n644\t        let rf = 1;\n645\t\n646\t        let mut node_shard_counts: std::collections::HashMap<String, usize> =\n647\t            std::collections::HashMap::new();\n648\t\n649\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n650\t            let assignment = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes, rf);\n651\t            if let Some(node) = assignment.first() {\n652\t                *node_shard_counts\n653\t                    .entry(node.as_str().to_string())\n654\t                    .or_insert(0) += 1;\n655\t            }\n656\t        }\n657\t\n658\t        // DoD requirement: each node holds 15–27 shards (accommodating hash distribution variance)\n659\t        for (node, count) in &node_shard_counts {\n660\t            assert!(\n661\t                *count >= 15 && *count <= 27,\n662\t                \"Node {node} has {count} shards, expected 15–27\"\n663\t            );\n664\t        }\n665\t\n666\t        // Total should equal shard_count\n667\t        let total: usize = node_shard_counts.values().sum();\n668\t        assert_eq!(total, shard_count as usize);\n669\t    }\n670\t\n671\t    // AT-5: RF=2 placement: top-2 nodes change minimally when a node is added or      .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n677\t            .collect();\n678\t        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n679\t            .into_iter()\n680\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n681\t            .collect();\n682\t\n683\t        let shard_count = 64;\n684\t        let rf = 2;\n685\t\n686\t        let mut changed_count = 0;\n687\t        for shard_id in 0..shard_count {\n688\t            let assign_3 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_3, rf);\n689\t            let assign_4 = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes_4, Tie-breaking on node_id for identical scores\n735\t    #[test]\n736\t    fn acceptance_tie_breaking_node_id() {\n737\t        // Create nodes that will have deterministic assignment\n738\t        let nodes: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node-a\", \"node-b\", \"node-c\"]\n739\t            .into_iter()\n740\t            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n741\t            .collect();\n742\t\n743\t        let rf = 3; // Request all nodes\n744\t        let shard_id = 42;\n745\t\n746\t        let assignment = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, &nodes, rf);\n747\t\n748\t        // Should return all nodes in acceptance_canonical_concatenation_order() {\n759\t        // Verify that score(shard_id, node_id) != score(node_id, shard_id)\n760\t        // by checking that different orders produce different results\n761\t        let shard_id = 42u32;\n762\t        let node_id = \"node1\";\n763\t\n764\t        let score_correct = score(shard_id, node_id);\n765\t\n766\t        // Compute score with reversed order (manually)\n767\t        use std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};\n768\t        let mut h_rev = twox_hash::XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n769\t        node_id.hash(&mut h_rev);\n770\t        shard_id.hash(&mut h_rev);\n771\t        let score_reversed = h_rev.finish();\n772\t\n773\t        // These should almost certainly be different\n774\t        assert_ne!(\n775\t }\n779\t}\n780\t"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"625a04e2-9b92-4bb8-9ea0-3bc46d48fb0c","uuid":"4b597a73-9082-417a-bc30-795754262da8","timestamp":"2026-05-09T19:19:58.338Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/router.rs","content":"//! Rendezvous hash-based routing and shard assignment.\n\nuse crate::topology::{Group, NodeId, Topology};\nuse std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};\nuse twox_hash::XxHash64;\n\n/// Compute a rendezvous score for a shard+node pair.\n///\n/// Higher scores win; used for deterministic shard assignment.\n///\n/// CRITICAL: Uses seed 0 to match Meilisearch Enterprise's hash function.\n/// Any deviation (different seed, different ordering, endianness) forks\n/// routing across any two Miroir instances and silently corrupts writes.\npub fn score(shard_id: u32, node_id: &str) -> u64 {\n    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n    shard_id.hash(&mut h);\n    node_id.hash(&mut h);\n    h.finish()\n}\n\n/// Assign a shard to `rf` nodes within a single replica group.\n///\n/// `group_nodes` is the subset of nodes belonging to that group.\n///\n/// Nodes are sorted by score descending, with ties broken lexicographically\n/// by node_id to ensure deterministic assignment even when hash scores collide.\npub fn assign_shard_in_group(shard_id: u32, group_nodes: &[NodeId], rf: usize) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    let mut scored: Vec<(u64, &NodeId)> = group_nodes\n        .iter()\n        .map(|n| (score(shard_id, n.as_str()), n))\n        .collect();\n    scored.sort_unstable_by(|a, b| {\n        b.0.cmp(&a.0)\n            .then_with(|| a.1.as_str().cmp(b.1.as_str()))\n    });\n    scored\n        .into_iter()\n        .take(rf)\n        .map(|(_, n)| n.clone())\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// All write targets for a document: the RF nodes in EACH replica group.\npub fn write_targets(shard_id: u32, topology: &Topology) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    topology\n        .groups()\n        .flat_map(|group| assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf()))\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// Select the replica group for a query (round-robin by query counter).\npub fn query_group(query_seq: u64, replica_groups: u32) -> u32 {\n    (query_seq % replica_groups as u64) as u32\n}\n\n/// The covering set for a search: one node per shard within the chosen group.\n///\n/// Returns a Vec where index i contains the node to query for shard i.\n/// The length is always exactly shard_count, even if multiple shards\n/// map to the same node.\npub fn covering_set(shard_count: u32, group: &Group, rf: usize, query_seq: u64) -> Vec<NodeId> {\n    (0..shard_count)\n        .map(|shard_id| {\n            let replicas = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), rf);\n            // rotate through replicas for intra-group load balancing\n            replicas[(query_seq as usize) % replicas.len()].clone()\n        })\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// Compute the shard ID for a document's primary key.\npub fn shard_for_key(primary_key: &str, shard_count: u32) -> u32 {\n    let mut h = XxHash64::with_seed(0);\n    primary_key.hash(&mut h);\n    (h.finish() % shard_count as u64) as u32\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n minimally when a node is added or removed\n    #[test]\n    fn acceptance_rf2_placement_stability() {\n        let nodes_3: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\"]\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|s| NodeId::new(s.to_string()))\n            .collect();\n        let nodes_4: Vec<NodeId> = vec![\"node1\", \"node2\", \"node3\", \"node4\"]\n            .into_iter()\n       // A change is if the intersection is less than RF\n            let intersection = set_3.intersection(&set_4).count();\n            if intersection < rf {\n                changed_count += 1;\n Request path.\n    pub path: String,\n}\n\n/// Response from a scatter operation.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ScatterResponse {\n    /// Responses from successful nodes.\n    pub responses: Vec<NodeResponse>,\n\n    /// Nodes that failed or timed out.\n    pub failed: Vec<NodeId>,\n}\n\n/// Response from a single node.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct NodeResponse {\n    /// Node     responses: Vec::new(),\n            failed: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        assert!(response.responses.is_empty());\n        assert!(response.failed.is_empty());\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn Strips `_rankingScore` if client didn't request it\n63\t/// 5. Always strips `_miroir_*` reserved fields\n64\t/// 6. Sums facet counts across shards\n65\t/// 7.        // Reverse<T> makes the \"smallest\" T become the \"largest\" Reverse<T>\n113\t        // So in BinaryHeap (max-heap), the smallest T ends up at the top\n114\t        use }\n1008\t}\n1009\t"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"625a04e2-9b92-4bb8-9ea0-3bc46d48fb0c","uuid":"dc045110-1a65-4c53-b346-bafa9a22985d","timestamp":"2026-05-09T19:20:04.121Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/merger.rs","content":"//! Result merger: combines shard results into a single response.\n\nuse crate::Result;\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse serde_json::Value;\nuse std::collections::{BTreeMap, BinaryHeap};\n\n/// Input to the merge function.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct MergeInput {\n    /// One page of hits per node in the covering set.\n    pub shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage>,\n\n    /// Offset to apply after merge.\n    pub offset: usize,\n\n    /// Limit to apply after merge.\n    pub limit: usize,\n\n    /// Whether the client requested the ranking score in the response.\n    pub client_requested_score: bool,\n\n    /// Facet names to include (if None, include all).\n    pub facets: Option<Vec<String>>,\n}\n\n/// A page of hits from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct ShardHitPage {\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct MergedSearchResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub estimated_total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n///\n/// This is the primary entry point for result merging. It:\n/// 1. Collects all hits with scores from all shards\n/// 2. Sorts globally by `_rankingScore` descending\n/// 3. Applies offset + limit after merge\n/// 4. Strips `_rankingScore` if client didn't request it\n/// 5. Always strips `_miroir_*` reserved fields\n/// 6. Sums facet counts across shards\n/// 7. Sums `estimatedTotalHits` across shards\n/// 8. Takes max `processingTimeMs` across shards\n///\n/// Uses a binary min-heap to avoid keeping all hits in RAM when fan-out is large.\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable facet serialization (deterministic JSON output).\npub fn merge(input: MergeInput) -> MergedSearchResult {\n    // Filter to only successful responses\n    let successful_shards: Vec<_> = input\n        .shard_hits\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|s| s.success)\n        .collect();\n\n    // Check if any shards failed (degraded mode)\n    let degraded = successful_shards.len() < input.shard_hits.len();\n\n    // Collect all hits with their ranking scores and primary keys\n    let mut all_hits: Vec<HitWithScore> = Vec::new();\n\n    for shard in &successful_shards {\n        if let Some(hits) = shard.body.get(\"hits\").and_then(|h| h.as_array()) {\n            for hit in hits {\n                let score = hit\n                    .get(\"_rankingScore\")\n                    .and_then(|s| s.as_f64())\n                    .unwrap_or(0.0);\n\n                let primary_key = hit\n                    .get(\"id\")\n                    .and_then(|id| id.as_str())\n                    .unwrap_or(\"\")\n                    .to_string();\n\n                all_hits.push(HitWithScore {\n                    score,\n                    primary_key,\n                    hit: hit.clone(),\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Use a min-heap of size offset + limit to avoid keeping all hits in RAM\n    let heap_size = input.offset + input.limit;\n    let top_hits = if all_hits.len() > heap_size * 2 {\n        // Only use heap optimization if we have significantly more hits than needed\n        // Use BinaryHeap with Reverse to get min-heap behavior\n        // Reverse<T> makes the \"smallest\" T become the \"largest\" Reverse<T>\n        // So in BinaryHeap (max-heap), the smallest T ends up at the top\n        use std::cmp::Reverse;\n\n        // First, define a wrapper with natural ascending order by score\n        #[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\n        struct AscendingHit(HitWithScore);\n\n        impl PartialOrd for AscendingHit {\n            fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n                Some(self.cmp(other))\n            }\n        }\n\n        impl Ord for AscendingHit {\n            fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n                // Ascending order: lower score first, then primary key ascending\n                match self.0.score.partial_cmp(&other.0.score) {\n                    Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n                        self.0.primary_key.cmp(&other.0.primary_key)\n                    }\n                    Some(ord) => ord,\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Reverse<AscendingHit> in BinaryHeap gives us a min-heap by score\n        // The lowest score (worst) will be at the top for easy replacement\n        let mut heap: BinaryHeap<Reverse<AscendingHit>> = BinaryHeap::new();\n\n        for hit in all_hits {\n            if heap.len() < heap_size {\n                heap.push(Reverse(AscendingHit(hit)));\n            } else {\n                // Peek at the smallest (worst) hit in our top-k\n                if let Some(Reverse(worst)) = heap.peek() {\n                    // If current hit is better than our worst, replace it\n                    // Compare using the score directly\n                    if hit.score > worst.0.score ||\n                       (hit.score == worst.0.score && hit.primary_key < worst.0.primary_key) {\n                        heap.pop();\n                        heap.push(Reverse(AscendingHit(hit)));\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Convert to sorted vector (descending by score)\n        let mut result: Vec<_> = heap.into_iter().map(|r| (r.0).0).collect();\n        result.sort_by(|a, b| a.descending_cmp(b));\n        result\n    } else {\n        // For smaller result sets, just sort directly\n        all_hits.sort_by(|a, b| a.descending_cmp(b));\n        all_hits\n    };\n\n    // Apply offset and limit\n    let page: Vec<Value> = top_hits\n        .into_iter()\n        .skip(input.offset)\n        .take(input.limit)\n        .map(|mut hit_with_score| {\n            let hit = &mut hit_with_score.hit;\n\n            // Strip all _miroir_* fields (always removed)\n            if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                obj.retain(|k, _| !k.starts_with(\"_miroir_\"));\n            }\n\n            // Strip _rankingScore if client didn't request it\n            if !input.client_requested_score {\n                if let Some(obj) = hit.as_object_mut() {\n                    obj.remove(\"_rankingScore\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            hit.clone()\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    // Aggregate facets across all shards\n    let facets = merge_facets(&successful_shards, input.facets.as_deref());\n\n    // Sum estimated total hits\n    let estimated_total_hits: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"estimatedTotalHits\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .sum();\n\n    // Max processing time across all shards\n    let processing_time_ms: u64 = successful_shards\n        .iter()\n        .filter_map(|s| s.body.get(\"processingTimeMs\").and_then(|v| v.as_u64()))\n        .max()\n        .unwrap_or(0);\n\n    MergedSearchResult {\n        hits: page,\n        facets,\n        estimated_total_hits,\n        processing_time_ms,\n        degraded,\n    }\n}\n\n/// A hit with its ranking score for sorting.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\nstruct HitWithScore {\n    score: f64,\n    primary_key: String,\n    hit: Value,\n}\n\nimpl PartialEq for HitWithScore {\n    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {\n        self.score == other.score && self.primary_key == other.primary_key\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Eq for HitWithScore {}\n\nimpl PartialOrd for HitWithScore {\n    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<std::cmp::Ordering> {\n        Some(self.cmp(other))\n    }\n}\n\nimpl HitWithScore {\n    /// Compare for descending order (score desc, primary key asc).\n    fn descending_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n        match other.score.partial_cmp(&self.score) {\n            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key ascending\n                self.primary_key.cmp(&other.primary_key)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl Ord for HitWithScore {\n    fn cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> std::cmp::Ordering {\n        // Sort by score descending, then by primary key ascending for tie-breaking\n        match self.score.partial_cmp(&other.score) {\n            Some(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal) | None => {\n                // On equal scores (or NaN), fall back to primary key\n                // Reversed for descending order\n                other.primary_key.cmp(&self.primary_key)\n            }\n            Some(ord) => ord.reverse(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Result merger: combines responses from multiple shards.\npub trait Merger: Send + Sync {\n    /// Merge search results from multiple shards.\n    ///\n    /// Takes the raw JSON responses from each shard and produces\n    /// a merged result with global sorting, offset/limit applied,\n    /// and facet aggregation.\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult>;\n}\n\n/// Response from a single shard.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ShardResponse {\n    /// Shard identifier.\n    pub shard_id: u32,\n\n    /// Raw JSON response from the node.\n    pub body: Value,\n\n    /// Whether this shard succeeded.\n    pub success: bool,\n}\n\n/// Merged search result (legacy, use MergedSearchResult instead).\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct MergedResult {\n    /// Merged hits (globally sorted, offset/limit applied).\n    pub hits: Vec<Value>,\n\n    /// Aggregated facets.\n    pub facets: Value,\n\n    /// Estimated total hits (sum of shard totals).\n    pub total_hits: u64,\n\n    /// Processing time in milliseconds.\n    pub processing_time_ms: u64,\n\n    /// Whether the response is degraded (some shards failed).\n    pub degraded: bool,\n}\n\n/// Default implementation of Merger.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct MergerImpl;\n\nimpl Merger for MergerImpl {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        offset: usize,\n        limit: usize,\n        client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        // Convert ShardResponse to ShardHitPage\n        let shard_hits: Vec<ShardHitPage> = shard_responses\n            .into_iter()\n            .map(|sr| ShardHitPage {\n                body: sr.body,\n                success: sr.success,\n            })\n            .collect();\n\n        // Call the new merge function\n        let input = MergeInput {\n            shard_hits,\n            offset,\n            limit,\n            client_requested_score,\n            facets: None,\n        };\n\n        let result = merge(input);\n\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: result.hits,\n            facets: result.facets,\n            total_hits: result.estimated_total_hits,\n            processing_time_ms: result.processing_time_ms,\n            degraded: result.degraded,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge facet distributions from all shards.\n///\n/// Facets are nested objects like `{\"color\": {\"red\": 10, \"blue\": 5}}`.\n/// We sum counts for each facet value across all shards.\n///\n/// Uses BTreeMap for stable, deterministic serialization.\nfn merge_facets(shards: &[&ShardHitPage], facet_filter: Option<&[String]>) -> Value {\n    let mut merged_facets: BTreeMap<String, BTreeMap<String, u64>> = BTreeMap::new();\n\n    for shard in shards {\n        if let Some(facets) = shard\n            .body\n            .get(\"facetDistribution\")\n            .and_then(|f| f.as_object())\n        {\n            for (facet_name, facet_values) in facets {\n                // Apply facet filter if provided\n                if let Some(filter) = facet_filter {\n                    if !filter.contains(&facet_name) {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(values_obj) = facet_values.as_object() {\n                    let entry = merged_facets.entry(facet_name.clone()).or_default();\n\n                    for (value, count) in values_obj {\n                        let count_val = count.as_u64().unwrap_or(0);\n                        *entry.entry(value.clone()).or_insert(0) += count_val;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Convert back to JSON structure (BTreeMap ensures stable key order)\n    let result: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = merged_facets\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|(facet_name, values)| {\n            let values_obj: serde_json::Map<String, Value> = values\n                .into_iter()\n                .map(|(k, v)| (k, Value::Number(v.into())))\n                .collect();\n            (facet_name, Value::Object(values_obj))\n        })\n        .collect();\n\n    Value::Object(result)\n}\n\n/// Stub implementation that returns empty results.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\npub struct StubMerger;\n\nimpl Merger for StubMerger {\n    fn merge(\n        &self,\n        _shard_responses: Vec<ShardResponse>,\n        _offset: usize,\n        _limit: usize,\n        _client_requested_score: bool,\n    ) -> Result<MergedResult> {\n        Ok(MergedResult {\n            hits: Vec::new(),\n            facets: serde_json::json!({}),\n            total_hits: 0,\n            processing_time_ms: 0,\n            degraded: false,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    fn create_hit(score: f64, id: &str) -> Value {\n        serde_json::json!({\n            \"id\": id,\n            \"_rankingScore\": score,\n            \"_miroir_shard\": 0,\n        })\n    }\n\n    fn create_shard_response(shard_id: u32, hits: Vec<Value>, total: u64) -> ShardResponse {\n        ShardResponse {\n            shard_id,\n            body: serde_json::json!({\n                \"hits\": hits,\n                \"estimatedTotalHits\": total,\n                \"processingTimeMs\": 10,\n                \"facetDistribution\": {},\n            }),\n            success: true,\n        }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_global_sort_by_ranking_score() {\n        let merger = MergerImpl;\n\n 10\n        let mut paged_ids = vec![];\n        for page in 0..5 {\n            let shards = vec![create_shard_response(0, hits.clone(), 50)];\n            let result = merger.merge(shards, page * .collect();\n\n        assert_eq!(paged_ids, all_ids);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_strip_all_miroir_reserved_fields() {\n        let merger = MergerImpl;\n\n        let hit = \"Test\",\n        });\n\n        let shards = vec![create_shard_response(0, vec![hit], 1)];\n\n        let result = merger.merge(shards, 0, 10, true).unwrap();\n\n        // _rankingScore should be
